class="Megamenu__MenuLinkText-sc-d700501a-3 jhaNnH">Media</span></a></li></ul></nav></nav></div></div></div></nav></div><div id="yle__contentAnchor" class="GridSystem-sc-aec765a1-2 innIAw"><div class="GridSystem__GridRow-sc-aec765a1-1 ArticlePage__ArticleRow-sc-d019dc0d-2 dDjXMO djOqhz"><main class="ArticlePage__ArticlePageMainColumn-sc-d019dc0d-0 aZYMy"><div class="GridSystem__GridCell-sc-aec765a1-0 ArticlePage__ArticleGridCell-sc-d019dc0d-1 gpkvrb fmDyMT"><div data-testid="article-wrapper" class="ArticleWrapper__Wrapper-sc-d40d1b2a-0 cKioCZ"><article class="yle__article arkki-theme-default" data-vrsproduct="uutiset"><header class="yle__article__header"><div class="sc-ptsiM FWzmu"><div class="ydscr__sc-1nj4haw-0 jEIKwb"><div class="ydscr__sc-1nj4haw-3 kmBeKZ"><div class="ydscr__sc-1nj4haw-5 iJxMaQ"><svg width="24" height="24" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true"><path fill="currentColor" d="M13.26 8c0-.69-.56-1.25-1.25-1.25H12a1.25 1.25 0 0 0 0 2.5h.01c.69 0 1.25-.56 1.25-1.25M12 11c-.55 0-1 .45-1 1v4c0 .55.45 1 1 1s1-.45 1-1v-4c0-.55-.45-1-1-1M12 1C5.92 1 1 5.92 1 12s4.92 11 11 11 11-4.92 11-11S18.08 1 12 1m0 20a9 9 0 1 1 .001-18.001A9 9 0 0 1 12 21"></path></svg></div><div class="ydscr__sc-1nj4haw-1 hXQNRP"><div class="ydscr__sc-1nj4haw-4 iPpFlK">The article is more than 9 years old</div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-gQUFyz jtbnbT"><a href="https://yle.fi/t/18-344678/en" aria-label="More articles on the topic The Finnish Broadcasting Company" class="ydscr__sc-w5hh4y-0 bCWgTJ sc-hLyRwt ZqtOv">The Finnish Broadcasting Company</a></div><h1 class="sc-iayzNI cnDeNE yle__article__heading yle__article__heading--1">Russian group behind 2013 Foreign Ministry hack</h1><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-edaYAx kCJIud eUUaaO yle__article__paragraph">The 2013 data hack at the Finnish Foreign Ministry was perpetrated by a group of Russian hackers, and was part of a wider campaign against targets in nearly fifty countries. Experts contacted by Yle have confirmed that the attack was perpetrated by the Turla group.</p><figure class="sc-kDXjwZ SBSRv yle__article__figure"><script type="application/ld+json">{"@id":"3-8591548","@context":"https://schema.org","image":{"@type":"ImageObject","description":"Tietoturvayritys arvioi, että Turla on iskenyt yhteensä satoihin kohteisiin lähes viidessäkymmenessä maassa.","copyrightHolder":"Jyrki Lyytikkä / Yle","url":"https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_2.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665"}}</script><div class="sc-ljKisr sc-UqUTu jYksOF jWZiTn"><div class="sc-eRJQtA chGiKH"><div class="sc-kieALA ytihg"><picture><source data-testid="source-for-S" media="(max-width: 767px)" srcSet="https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_2.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 2x,https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_1.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 1x"/><source data-testid="source-for-M" media="(min-width: 768px)" srcSet="https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_357,w_636/dpr_2.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 2x,https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777910232544,c_fill,g_faces,h_357,w_636/dpr_1.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665 1x"/><img alt="Tietoliikennejohtoja." src="https://images.cdn.yle.fi/image/upload/ar_1.7777777777777777,c_fill,g_faces,h_431,w_767/dpr_1.0/q_auto:eco/f_auto/fl_lossy/13-3-7284665" class="sc-dibcMh cYuCkg"/></picture></div><div class="sc-bFwXsg kupnSS"><button aria-disabled="false" aria-busy="false" class="ydscr__sc-17sr1bx-0 ydscr__sc-17sr1bx-2 fLisnE dmhQqn"><span class="ydscr__sc-17sr1bx-7 fnwKQz yds-button__content">Open image viewer</span></button></div></div></div><figcaption class="sc-fIQtvO GJmSi"><span>Tietoturvayritys arvioi, että Turla on iskenyt yhteensä satoihin kohteisiin lähes viidessäkymmenessä maassa.</span><span> <!-- -->Image: Jyrki Lyytikkä / Yle</span></figcaption></figure><div class="sc-dMIikG gGAXtk"><div class="sc-cPTlUd bUcZrl yle__article__date"><time class="sc-gvBaNG bZnMrC yle__article__date--published" dateTime="2016-01-13T13:21:26+02:00">13.1.2016 13:21</time><span aria-hidden="true" class="sc-dJjnMf cmrhaB">•</span><time class="sc-gvBaNG bZnMrC yle__article__date--modified" dateTime="2016-01-14T07:58:44+02:00">Updated<!-- --> <!-- -->14.1.2016 7:58</time></div></div></header><section class="yle__article__content"><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">In 2013 Finland’s Foreign Ministry had its systems hacked by what investigators described as ‘a state actor’. Now Yle&#x27;s sources have confirmed who was behind the attack: the Turla group of Russian-speaking hackers who perpetrated attacks on targets in more than 50 countries worldwide during the same period.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">Stefan Tanase of Kaspersky security says that the Turla group is the premier Russian hacker organization—and it targets ministries, embassies and militaries in Russia’s neighbours. </p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">&quot;We believe that the Turla group is a nation state-sponsored attacker,&quot; said Tanase. &quot;We have seen traces in their malware and their servers, which we analyse, that point to the fact that the authors are Russian speaking and they definitely seem to have lot of resources to their cyber-espionage operation.&quot;</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">Yle has confirmed from several European sources that the 2013 attacks on the Foreign Ministry were perpetrated by the Turla group. The Foreign Ministry says that it has investigated the attacks in the light of similar actions targeting other nation states around Russia.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">&quot;The typical signs in these attack tools can be observed once you get to the stage where you know what you’re looking for and can check to see if there’s anything like that, and if there have been any changes in their tools,&quot; said Ari Uusikartano of the Foreign Ministry.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">Uusikartano says that the attack by Turla hit most countries in western Europe. Kaspersky, which published a report on the methods and targets of Turla (which did not at the time mention Finland) last autumn, has outlined the methods used by the attackers.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">First, cyber spies start by gathering information about the target via sources like social media, public websites and internal phone directories.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">Second, they choose a few employees to whom they send emails which include a link to an apparently interesting website, which appears to be connected somehow to the targets everyday life or area of specialization. The hackers have however embedded malware in the site concerned.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">Third, when the employee visits the site, the malware ends up on his or her computer.</p><p class="sc-jSJJpv sc-cnVfeA kCJIud hhUzkn yle__article__paragraph">That allows in the attacker, as happened to the Finnish Foreign Ministry in 2013. The ministry says it&#x27;s learned it&#x27;s lessons from this attack--but the hackers may already have moved on to a new method.</p></section><footer class="yle__article__footer"><div
